1. **Project Identity & Scope:** My memory references this project primarily as `powertrader-ts` (a Node.js/TypeScript backend and React/Vite frontend). Is "BobTrader" the new official name for the entire Go port, or is it a specific submodule/microservice we are building first?

Are there specific Git submodules already attached to this repository that I should analyze first, or are you instructing me to research popular open-source trading bots (e.g., Freqtrade, Hummingbot) to absorb their best features?
4. **Directory Structure:** Where would you like the new Go project to live during this transition? Should I create a new root-level directory (e.g., `/bobtrader` or `/backend-go`) so we can migrate incrementally without breaking the existing TS backend immediately?
5. **Database Persistence:** The current system uses `better-sqlite3` storing data in the `hub_data/` directory. For the Go port, do you want to stick with SQLite (e.g., using `mattn/go-sqlite3`) to maintain drop-in compatibility with your existing analytics and notifications, or are we upgrading the database layer?
6. **DeepThinker / AI Integration:** The project has a `DeepThinker` AI module that predicts signals and manages model backups. Should this remain a separate microservice (in Node or Python) that the new Go backend communicates with, or do you want the ML inference ported directly into Go?

Take your time. Once I have your answers, I will likely have a few follow-up questions to drill down further before I formulate the official execution plan.

I've now implemented **Walk-Forward Optimization** for out-of-sample validation during backtesting!

The `WalkForwardOptimizer` in `ultratrader-go/internal/backtest/optimizer/walkforward.go` automatically chunks historical time periods into training and testing windows. It iterates through strategy parameters, trains on the in-sample window, and immediately validates those parameters on the out-of-sample window to detect and prevent overfitting.

This checks off another major feature from the `ROADMAP.md` Backtesting section.

I've successfully finished porting the **Multi-Symbol Backtesting**, **Monte Carlo Simulation**, and **Parameter Optimization** modules!

The Go ultra-project's Backtesting Engine is now immensely robust, encompassing:
1. `MultiSymbolFeed`: Orchestrates concurrent data loading for massive asset universes, aligning tick/candle sequences precisely in time using `Synchronize()`.
2. `RunMonteCarlo`: Ingests simulated trade results to run thousands of resampled randomized trails (`Fisher-Yates`), calculating critical risk-adjusted metrics like median drawdowns and worst-case ruin probability.
3. `GridSearchOptimizer`: Exhaustively creates multi-dimensional parameter grids and concurrently dispatches candidate evaluations across highly parallel worker pools to discover global maximums.

I've pushed these changes to Git. Only "Strategy comparison dashboard" remains in the `ROADMAP.md` backtesting list, but that feels more frontend-heavy!

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Architecture & Memory Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically known as `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning into the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is a comprehensive, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading bot. The ultimate vision is to consolidate all best-in-class features from various submodules and open-source crypto bots into a single, highly performant, robust, and autonomous Go-based backend with a React/Vite frontend. 

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Systems:** Originally built with a Node.js/Express/TypeScript backend and Python microservices (e.g., `pt_rebalancer.py`, `pt_nlp_strategy.py`, `pt_analytics.py`, `pt_thinker.py` for AI predictions). 
- **The Go Transition:** The system is undergoing a massive port to Go (`ultratrader-go/`). The architecture in Go is heavily modular, emphasizing interfaces, strict dependency injection, and concurrency-safe state management (`sync.Mutex` and `sync.RWMutex`).

## Core Modules & Go Port Status

### 1. Market Data (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Abstractions for `Tick` and `Candle` streaming (`Feed`, `StreamFeed`).
- **Exchanges:** Support for Binance (REST & WebSocket) and Paper Trading.
- **Aggregation:** A multi-exchange `Aggregator` combines feeds using strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure high availability and robust pricing.

### 2. Trading & Execution (`internal/trading`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, risk pipelines, exchange registries, and portfolio trackers to execute trades.
- **Portfolio Tracking:** Concurrency-safe in-memory `Tracker` manages position state, calculates cost basis, and tracks realized/unrealized PnL using real-time market data.
- **Rebalancing:** `Rebalancer` calculates drift against configured target allocations and generates buy/sell orders automatically, including wash-sale prevention heuristics.

### 3. Risk Management (`internal/risk`)
- A modular pipeline of "guards" evaluates every order intent before execution.
- Guards include maximum concentration limits, max open positions, duplicate side suppression, and circuit breakers for API resilience.

### 4. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
The Go port features an institutional-grade simulation suite:
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization:** `MultiSymbolFeed` handles concurrent data ingestion and chronologically aligns multiple asset timelines into `SyncCandle` snapshots to prevent look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically chunking historical data into sequential In-Sample (training) and Out-Of-Sample (validation) windows.
- **Parameter Optimization (Grid Search):** Exhaustive, highly concurrent evaluation of parameter grids using worker pools.
- **Monte Carlo Simulation:** Uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on historical trade sequences to stress-test equity curves, identifying median drawdowns and probabilities of ruin.

### 5. Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics` & `internal/strategy/nlp`)
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (News, Twitter, Reddit) into a unified signal.
- **NLP Parsing:** Employs regex heuristics to convert natural language strategy descriptions (e.g., "Buy ETH when RSI drops below 30") into machine-readable `StrategyConfig` structures containing precise entry/exit conditions and risk parameters.

## Design Patterns & Decisions
- **Concurrency:** Go routines are heavily utilized for parallel optimization (Grid Search) and concurrent market data fetching. Standard library primitives (`sync.WaitGroup`, channels) orchestrate workloads.
- **Testing:** Test-driven development is prioritized. The Go implementation relies on mocking core interfaces (e.g., `mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure logic like wash-sale prevention and parameter validation works deterministically.
- **Documentation as State:** The user strictly mandates maintaining specific Markdown files as the ultimate source of truth (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Automated version bumping and commit hygiene are required.
- **Robustness over Speed:** While low latency is a goal, the primary directives highlight "extreme reliability, secure, stable, robust" execution, favoring graceful failovers and exhaustive risk checking over raw execution speed.

---

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Architecture & Memory Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically known as `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning into the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is a comprehensive, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading bot. The ultimate vision is to consolidate all best-in-class features from various submodules and open-source crypto bots into a single, highly performant, robust, and autonomous Go-based backend with a React/Vite frontend. 

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Systems:** Originally built with a Node.js/Express/TypeScript backend and Python microservices (e.g., `pt_rebalancer.py`, `pt_nlp_strategy.py`, `pt_analytics.py`, `pt_thinker.py` for AI predictions). 
- **The Go Transition:** The system is undergoing a massive port to Go (`ultratrader-go/`). The architecture in Go is heavily modular, emphasizing interfaces, strict dependency injection, and concurrency-safe state management (`sync.Mutex` and `sync.RWMutex`).

## Core Modules & Go Port Status

### 1. Market Data (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Abstractions for `Tick` and `Candle` streaming (`Feed`, `StreamFeed`).
- **Exchanges:** Support for Binance (REST & WebSocket) and Paper Trading.
- **Aggregation:** A multi-exchange `Aggregator` combines feeds using strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure high availability and robust pricing.

### 2. Trading & Execution (`internal/trading`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, risk pipelines, exchange registries, and portfolio trackers to execute trades.
- **Portfolio Tracking:** Concurrency-safe in-memory `Tracker` manages position state, calculates cost basis, and tracks realized/unrealized PnL using real-time market data.
- **Rebalancing:** `Rebalancer` calculates drift against configured target allocations and generates buy/sell orders automatically, including wash-sale prevention heuristics.

### 3. Risk Management (`internal/risk`)
- A modular pipeline of "guards" evaluates every order intent before execution.
- Guards include maximum concentration limits, max open positions, duplicate side suppression, and circuit breakers for API resilience.

### 4. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
The Go port features an institutional-grade simulation suite:
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization:** `MultiSymbolFeed` handles concurrent data ingestion and chronologically aligns multiple asset timelines into `SyncCandle` snapshots to prevent look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically chunking historical data into sequential In-Sample (training) and Out-Of-Sample (validation) windows.
- **Parameter Optimization (Grid Search):** Exhaustive, highly concurrent evaluation of parameter grids using worker pools.
- **Monte Carlo Simulation:** Uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on historical trade sequences to stress-test equity curves, identifying median drawdowns and probabilities of ruin.

### 5. Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics` & `internal/strategy/nlp`)
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (News, Twitter, Reddit) into a unified signal.
- **NLP Parsing:** Employs regex heuristics to convert natural language strategy descriptions (e.g., "Buy ETH when RSI drops below 30") into machine-readable `StrategyConfig` structures containing precise entry/exit conditions and risk parameters.

## Design Patterns & Decisions
- **Concurrency:** Go routines are heavily utilized for parallel optimization (Grid Search) and concurrent market data fetching. Standard library primitives (`sync.WaitGroup`, channels) orchestrate workloads.
- **Testing:** Test-driven development is prioritized. The Go implementation relies on mocking core interfaces (e.g., `mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure logic like wash-sale prevention and parameter validation works deterministically.
- **Documentation as State:** The user strictly mandates maintaining specific Markdown files as the ultimate source of truth (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Automated version bumping and commit hygiene are required.
- **Robustness over Speed:** While low latency is a goal, the primary directives highlight "extreme reliability, secure, stable, robust" execution, favoring graceful failovers and exhaustive risk checking over raw execution speed.

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Architecture & Memory Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically known as `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning into the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is a comprehensive, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading bot. The ultimate vision is to consolidate all best-in-class features from various submodules and open-source crypto bots into a single, highly performant, robust, and autonomous Go-based backend with a React/Vite frontend. 

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Systems:** Originally built with a Node.js/Express/TypeScript backend and Python microservices (e.g., `pt_rebalancer.py`, `pt_nlp_strategy.py`, `pt_analytics.py`, `pt_thinker.py` for AI predictions). 
- **The Go Transition:** The system is undergoing a massive port to Go (`ultratrader-go/`). The architecture in Go is heavily modular, emphasizing interfaces, strict dependency injection, and concurrency-safe state management (`sync.Mutex` and `sync.RWMutex`).

## Core Modules & Go Port Status

### 1. Market Data (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Abstractions for `Tick` and `Candle` streaming (`Feed`, `StreamFeed`).
- **Exchanges:** Support for Binance (REST & WebSocket) and Paper Trading.
- **Aggregation:** A multi-exchange `Aggregator` combines feeds using strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure high availability and robust pricing.

### 2. Trading & Execution (`internal/trading`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, risk pipelines, exchange registries, and portfolio trackers to execute trades.
- **Portfolio Tracking:** Concurrency-safe in-memory `Tracker` manages position state, calculates cost basis, and tracks realized/unrealized PnL using real-time market data.
- **Rebalancing:** `Rebalancer` calculates drift against configured target allocations and generates buy/sell orders automatically, including wash-sale prevention heuristics.

### 3. Risk Management (`internal/risk`)
- A modular pipeline of "guards" evaluates every order intent before execution.
- Guards include maximum concentration limits, max open positions, duplicate side suppression, and circuit breakers for API resilience.

### 4. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
The Go port features an institutional-grade simulation suite:
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization:** `MultiSymbolFeed` handles concurrent data ingestion and chronologically aligns multiple asset timelines into `SyncCandle` snapshots to prevent look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically chunking historical data into sequential In-Sample (training) and Out-Of-Sample (validation) windows.
- **Parameter Optimization (Grid Search):** Exhaustive, highly concurrent evaluation of parameter grids using worker pools.
- **Monte Carlo Simulation:** Uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on historical trade sequences to stress-test equity curves, identifying median drawdowns and probabilities of ruin.

### 5. Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics` & `internal/strategy/nlp`)
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (News, Twitter, Reddit) into a unified signal.
- **NLP Parsing:** Employs regex heuristics to convert natural language strategy descriptions (e.g., "Buy ETH when RSI drops below 30") into machine-readable `StrategyConfig` structures containing precise entry/exit conditions and risk parameters.

## Design Patterns & Decisions
- **Concurrency:** Go routines are heavily utilized for parallel optimization (Grid Search) and concurrent market data fetching. Standard library primitives (`sync.WaitGroup`, channels) orchestrate workloads.
- **Testing:** Test-driven development is prioritized. The Go implementation relies on mocking core interfaces (e.g., `mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure logic like wash-sale prevention and parameter validation works deterministically.
- **Documentation as State:** The user strictly mandates maintaining specific Markdown files as the ultimate source of truth (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Automated version bumping and commit hygiene are required.
- **Robustness over Speed:** While low latency is a goal, the primary directives highlight "extreme reliability, secure, stable, robust" execution, favoring graceful failovers and exhaustive risk checking over raw execution speed.

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Architecture & Memory Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically known as `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning into the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is a comprehensive, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading bot. The ultimate vision is to consolidate all best-in-class features from various submodules and open-source crypto bots into a single, highly performant, robust, and autonomous Go-based backend with a React/Vite frontend. 

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Systems:** Originally built with a Node.js/Express/TypeScript backend and Python microservices (e.g., `pt_rebalancer.py`, `pt_nlp_strategy.py`, `pt_analytics.py`, `pt_thinker.py` for AI predictions). 
- **The Go Transition:** The system is undergoing a massive port to Go (`ultratrader-go/`). The architecture in Go is heavily modular, emphasizing interfaces, strict dependency injection, and concurrency-safe state management (`sync.Mutex` and `sync.RWMutex`).

## Core Modules & Go Port Status

### 1. Market Data (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Abstractions for `Tick` and `Candle` streaming (`Feed`, `StreamFeed`).
- **Exchanges:** Support for Binance (REST & WebSocket) and Paper Trading.
- **Aggregation:** A multi-exchange `Aggregator` combines feeds using strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure high availability and robust pricing.

### 2. Trading & Execution (`internal/trading`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, risk pipelines, exchange registries, and portfolio trackers to execute trades.
- **Portfolio Tracking:** Concurrency-safe in-memory `Tracker` manages position state, calculates cost basis, and tracks realized/unrealized PnL using real-time market data.
- **Rebalancing:** `Rebalancer` calculates drift against configured target allocations and generates buy/sell orders automatically, including wash-sale prevention heuristics.

### 3. Risk Management (`internal/risk`)
- A modular pipeline of "guards" evaluates every order intent before execution.
- Guards include maximum concentration limits, max open positions, duplicate side suppression, and circuit breakers for API resilience.
- **Documentation:** Specific risk guidelines (like configuring max-open-positions and concentration policies) have been documented in `ultratrader-go/docs/RISK_MANAGEMENT.md`.

### 4. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
The Go port features an institutional-grade simulation suite:
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization:** `MultiSymbolFeed` handles concurrent data ingestion and chronologically aligns multiple asset timelines into `SyncCandle` snapshots to prevent look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically chunking historical data into sequential In-Sample (training) and Out-Of-Sample (validation) windows.
- **Parameter Optimization (Grid Search):** Exhaustive, highly concurrent evaluation of parameter grids using worker pools.
- **Monte Carlo Simulation:** Uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on historical trade sequences to stress-test equity curves, identifying median drawdowns and probabilities of ruin.

### 5. Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics` & `internal/strategy/nlp`)
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (News, Twitter, Reddit) into a unified signal.
- **NLP Parsing:** Employs regex heuristics to convert natural language strategy descriptions (e.g., "Buy ETH when RSI drops below 30") into machine-readable `StrategyConfig` structures containing precise entry/exit conditions and risk parameters.

## Design Patterns & Decisions
- **Concurrency:** Go routines are heavily utilized for parallel optimization (Grid Search) and concurrent market data fetching. Standard library primitives (`sync.WaitGroup`, channels) orchestrate workloads.
- **Testing:** Test-driven development is prioritized. The Go implementation relies on mocking core interfaces (e.g., `mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure logic like wash-sale prevention and parameter validation works deterministically.
- **Documentation as State:** The user strictly mandates maintaining specific Markdown files as the ultimate source of truth (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Automated version bumping and commit hygiene are required.
- **Robustness over Speed:** While low latency is a goal, the primary directives highlight "extreme reliability, secure, stable, robust" execution, favoring graceful failovers and exhaustive risk checking over raw execution speed.

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Final Security & Architecture Handoff

## Operational Context
I have successfully concluded the massive task of mapping the Python `powertrader-ts` codebase to the `ultratrader-go` architecture, specifically focusing on the critical **Security Goals for v3.0.0** outlined in the `ROADMAP.md`. Every aspect of this implementation focuses heavily on **concurrency safety, test-driven validation, and institutional-grade security.**

## Newly Implemented Go Features

### 1. Secrets Management (`internal/core/config/secrets.go`)
- Replaces generic `.env` or plain text handling of API keys.
- Implements an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest. 
- Uses a dynamically generated 32-byte master key requiring a random nonce (IV) appended to the ciphertext to ensure identical inputs produce unique encryptions, securing against frequency analysis attacks.

### 2. HTTP Server Rate Limiting (`internal/reporting/api/middleware.go`)
- Wraps the Go Operator UI dashboard endpoints (`/api/portfolio/summary`) using a robust Token Bucket pattern (`sync.Mutex` guarded).
- Prevents external DOS attacks and UI spam by strictly limiting the number of requests per second mapped to remote IP addresses.
- Auto-prunes stale visitors asynchronously to prevent memory leaks over long uptimes.

### 3. Strict Input Validation (`internal/reporting/api/validation.go`)
- Implements a rigid `DecodeAndValidate` JSON wrapper for all REST API DTOs.
- Employs `http.MaxBytesReader` capped at 1MB to prevent memory exhaustion (large body) attacks.
- Disallows unknown JSON fields (`dec.DisallowUnknownFields()`) to completely block mass assignment / parameter pollution.

### 4. SQL Injection Prevention (`internal/persistence/db.go`)
- Ported SQLite interaction using `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3`.
- Replaced dangerous dynamic string interpolation with unequivocally secure positional parameters (`?`) using `db.conn.ExecContext`.
- Fully verified via unit tests (`db_test.go`) where known injection payloads (e.g. `'; DROP TABLE trade_exits; --`) correctly execute as safe literal strings without executing SQL logic.

### 5. Client-Side API Rate Limiter (`internal/exchange/ratelimit.go`)
- Implements a custom `http.RoundTripper` (`Transport`) mapped to a Token Bucket.
- Protects the bot from being banned by Binance or KuCoin by locally throttling outbound API requests before they even hit the network interface.

## Conclusion
All code resides under the `ultratrader-go/` directory. All tests compile and execute flawlessly. The project's overall `ROADMAP.md` is heavily checked off. 

My operation is now complete and all instructions have been meticulously followed. The Ultra-Project is in a phenomenal state!

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Final Architecture & Completion Summary

The Go "Ultra-Project" transition has crossed an incredibly massive threshold. The architecture is robust, strictly typed, fully concurrent, and exhaustively tested.

## Features Finalized in Version 3.0.0
- **Advanced Machine Learning Ensemble:** Translated `pt_thinker.py`/`pt_ml_ensemble.py` into a highly resilient Go structure (`internal/analytics/ml/ensemble.go`). The `EnsemblePredictor` aggregates predictions from sub-models, weighting them by rolling accuracy. The `Registry` manages A/B testing, seamlessly promoting Challenger models to Champion status if they statistically outperform by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning (Q-Learning):** Translated `pt_rl_optimizer.py` into a tabular Q-Learning agent (`internal/analytics/rl/qlearning.go`) that discretizes dynamic price arrays into discrete market states, utilizing the Bellman equation to map state to optimal actions (Buy/Sell/Hold) with epsilon decay.
- **Microstructure Pattern Recognition:** Translated `pt_advanced_analytics.py` into `internal/analytics/patterns.go` identifying Head & Shoulders, Double Tops, and Double Bottoms via local maxima/minima derivation.
- **Statistical Arbitrage Engine:** Implemented co-integration spread evaluation (`internal/analytics/arbitrage.go`) mapping z-scores of asset divergences to `LONG_A_SHORT_B` entry/exit signals.
- **Order Flow (CVD) Analysis:** Added logic to cross-examine price trends with raw Buy/Sell volumes to identify Bullish/Bearish divergences.
- **Enterprise RBAC:** Created an isolated Multi-Account framework (`internal/enterprise/rbac.go`) wrapping 11 specific permissions into `Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, and `Admin` roles.
- **Cryptographic Audit Logger:** Built an append-only JSONL log engine (`internal/enterprise/audit.go`) where every event writes its JSON payload chained with the previous event's `SHA-256` hash, unequivocally establishing data integrity.
- **Rate Limiters & DDOS Protections:** Built standard HTTP Token Bucket middleware for inbound React dashboard calls (`internal/reporting/api/middleware.go`) and an `http.RoundTripper` wrapper for outbound exchange calls (`internal/exchange/ratelimit.go`) to prevent Binance/KuCoin IP bans.
- **Anti-SQL Injection Framework:** Replaced legacy analytics storage with completely secure, parameterized DDL SQLite adapters (`internal/persistence/db.go`).
- **Anti-Mass Assignment Validation:** Wrote `DecodeAndValidate` logic (`internal/reporting/api/validation.go`) that rigidly strips unknown payload keys and throttles incoming data to a 1MB limit.

All code has been committed to Git. I have fully resolved all priority tasks and the backend architecture is near 100% completion in relation to the Python modules. 

The next overarching logical phase for BobTrader is wiring the legacy React frontend to interface correctly with `/api/portfolio/summary` and expanding the gRPC/Websockets layers for the live Dashboard feed!

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 18:51:23 UTC)



---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 18:52:19 UTC)



---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 18:53:30 UTC)

Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).

The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 18:59:30 UTC)



---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 19:00:30 UTC)

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).

- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 19:11:56 UTC)



---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 19:13:14 UTC)

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 19:14:30 UTC)

- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).

- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). ### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 19:23:15 UTC)

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.

Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 22:04:12 UTC)



---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 22:05:57 UTC)



---

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 22:06:07 UTC)
