# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.

Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. ## Core Modules & Subsystems

- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

### Agent (Sun, 12 Apr 2026 23:59:48 UTC)

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:00:16 UTC)



---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:00:54 UTC)

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). - **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:06:36 UTC)



---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:08:07 UTC)

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:08:11 UTC)

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:09:16 UTC)



---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:10:49 UTC)

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:23:57 UTC)



---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:25:37 UTC)



---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:25:59 UTC)

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:26:17 UTC)



---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 00:27:12 UTC)

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 01:17:39 UTC)

[PROJECT_MEMORY]

# BobTrader / PowerTrader-TS Comprehensive Architecture & Decisions Summary

## Overview & Vision
The project (historically `powertrader-ts`, now transitioning to the `BobTrader` / `ultratrader-go` "Ultra-Project") is an advanced, highly modular, multi-exchange cryptocurrency trading engine. The ultimate goal is to fuse the best features of popular open-source bots with custom, institutional-grade analytics into a high-performance Go backend, paired with a modern React/Vite web dashboard.

## Architectural Evolution
- **Legacy Stack:** Initially built around a Node.js/TypeScript backend and numerous Python microservices (`pt_*.py`) that handled AI prediction, analytics, risk management, and natural language processing.
- **The Go Transition (`ultratrader-go/`):** The system has been almost entirely ported to Go. The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 1. Market Data & Aggregation (`internal/marketdata`)
- **Feeds:** Utilizes `Feed` and `StreamFeed` interfaces for abstracting historical candles and live ticks.
- **Aggregator:** Combines multiple exchange feeds (e.g., Binance, KuCoin, Paper) into a single, unified price source. It supports strategies like `AveragePrice`, `MedianPrice`, and `Failover` to ensure robust, uninterrupted pricing.

### 2. Trading, Portfolio & Risk (`internal/trading`, `internal/risk`)
- **Execution Service:** Tightly couples accounts, exchange registries, and risk pipelines. 
- **Portfolio Tracker:** Concurrency-safe in-memory store that tracks realized/unrealized PnL and calculates cost basis dynamically using live market feeds.
- **Rebalancer:** Monitors portfolio drift against target allocations and autonomously generates `Buy`/`Sell` orders. It features a critical **Wash Sale Prevention** heuristic that blocks selling assets at a loss if they were purchased within 30 days.
- **Risk Guards:** Every order passes through a pipeline of "guards":
  - *Max Positions:* Limits concurrent open trades.
  - *Max Concentration:* Blocks orders that would push a single asset beyond a specified percentage of total portfolio value.
  - *Duplicate Side Suppression:* Prevents algorithmic bugs from spamming the same side of an order book.

### 3. Backtesting & Simulation (`internal/backtest`)
- **Multi-Symbol Synchronization (`MultiSymbolFeed`):** Concurrently loads historical data and chronologically aligns multiple assets into `SyncCandle` snapshots, entirely preventing look-ahead bias.
- **Walk-Forward Optimization:** Mitigates overfitting by dynamically dividing history into sequential training (In-Sample) and validation (Out-Of-Sample) windows.
- **Grid Search & Monte Carlo:** Exhaustively evaluates strategy parameters concurrently, and uses Fisher-Yates shuffling on trade sequences to stress-test equity curves (calculating median drawdowns and ruin probability).

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.
- **Reinforcement Learning:** Tabular Q-Learning agent that discretizes price features into states and learns optimal actions via the Bellman equation with epsilon decay.
- **Pattern Recognition & Order Flow:** Algorithms to detect Double Tops, Head & Shoulders, and Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) divergences (Bullish/Bearish).
- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.
- **Sentiment Engine:** Aggregates and clamps sentiment scores from external providers (e.g., Twitter, News).

### 5. Enterprise & Security (`internal/enterprise`, `internal/core`, `internal/persistence`)
- **Secrets Management:** Discards `.env` files for an AES-GCM engine that encrypts API keys at rest.
- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.

---

### Agent (Mon, 13 Apr 2026 01:19:13 UTC)

The overarching design philosophy is strict modularity, heavy use of interfaces for dependency injection, and concurrency-safe data structures (`sync.Mutex` / `sync.RWMutex`) to handle high-frequency tick data.

## Core Modules & Subsystems

### 4. Advanced Analytics & AI (`internal/analytics`)
- **ML Ensemble & Model Registry:** A weighted voting system that combines multiple predictive models based on their rolling accuracy. A `Registry` manages A/B testing, promoting a "Challenger" model to "Champion" if it outperforms by >5%.

- **Statistical Arbitrage:** Calculates Pearson correlation, spread means, and Z-Scores to identify `LONG_A_SHORT_B` mean-reversion pair trading opportunities.

- **Rate Limiting:** Implements Token Bucket algorithms both for *inbound* API requests (protecting the Web Dashboard) and *outbound* `http.RoundTripper` transports (preventing exchange API bans).
- **Input Validation:** Strict JSON decoding (`DecodeAndValidate`) that enforces 1MB body limits and disallows unknown fields to prevent mass assignment attacks.
- **SQL Injection Prevention:** Utilizes `github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3` with strictly parameterized `?` queries.
- **Multi-Account RBAC:** Enforces strict boundaries across 11 permissions spanning 4 roles (`Viewer`, `Trader`, `Manager`, `Admin`).
- **Cryptographic Audit Log:** Writes system events to an append-only JSONL file where every entry contains a `SHA-256` hash of the current payload chained with the previous entry's hash.

## Design Decisions & Development Patterns
1. **Concurrency First:** The Go port leverages Goroutines extensively—whether it's `sync.WaitGroup` for multi-symbol data fetching or worker pools for parameter grid optimization.
2. **Test-Driven:** The architecture relies heavily on mocked interfaces (`mockFeed`, `mockOptEvaluator`) to ensure complex logic (like wash sale prevention or grid search combinatorics) behaves deterministically.
3. **Documentation as State:** Project health is strictly managed via a suite of markdown files (`TODO.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `VERSION.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `AGENTS.md`). Updates to features *must* be reflected in these files alongside semantic version bumps (currently at **v3.0.0**).
4. **Reliability Over Raw Speed:** The system prioritizes graceful failovers, robust input validation, and exhaustive pre-execution risk checks over microsecond latency.

## Next Strategic Steps
The backend architecture is nearly 100% complete in relation to the legacy Python modules. The next major phase is hooking the **React/Vite frontend** into the newly secured Go REST APIs (e.g., `/api/portfolio/summary`) and extending Go's `gorilla/websocket` implementation to stream live `SyncCandle` data and model predictions directly to the UI.
